    { 1100409092;;DataItem;BaseServiceInspectionList;
               DataItemTable=Table11071930;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Code)
                                 WHERE(Visible for Field Service=CONST(Yes));
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ServiceInspectionVersion@1100409000 : Record 11071750;
                                  ServiceInspectionManagement@1100409001 : Codeunit 11012844;
                                BEGIN
                                  ServiceInspectionVersion.SETRANGE("Inspection Type", ServiceInspectionVersion."Inspection Type"::"Base Inspection List");
                                  ServiceInspectionVersion.SETRANGE(Code, Code);
                                  ServiceInspectionVersion.SETFILTER("Index Date", '..%1', TODAY);
                                  IF ServiceInspectionVersion.ISEMPTY THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  TempServiceInspectionLine.RESET;
                                  TempServiceInspectionLine.DELETEALL;

                                  ServiceInspectionManagement.CollectTmpInspVersionLines(
                                    TempServiceInspectionLine."Inspection Type"::"Base Inspection List", '', Code, '', '', TODAY,
                                    TempServiceInspectionLine."Inspection Type"::"Base Inspection List", '', Code, '', '', FALSE, TempServiceInspectionLine);
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    BEGIN
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillTempCompany@1100409000();
    VAR
      Company@1100409000 : Record 2000000006;
      MobileSetup@1100409001 : Record 11012676;
      CompanyPlanGroup@1100525000 : Record 11229300;
    BEGIN
      IF Company.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF CompanyPlanGroup.BelongsCompanyToCurrentCompanyPlanGroup(Company.Name) THEN BEGIN
            MobileSetup.CHANGECOMPANY(Company.Name);
            IF MobileSetup.GET THEN
              IF MobileSetup."4PS-Mobile Active" THEN BEGIN
                TempCompany.COPY(Company);
                TempCompany.INSERT;
              END;
          END;
        UNTIL Company.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillTempCostObject@1100409001();
    VAR
      CostObject@1100409000 : Record 349;
      GeneralLedgerSetup@1100409001 : Record 98;
      Resource@1100409002 : Record 11229278;
      ExportFilterSetMgtMobile@1100409003 : Codeunit 11012200;
    BEGIN
      GeneralLedgerSetup.GET;
      GeneralLedgerSetup.TESTFIELD("Global Dimension 2 Code");

      TempCostObject.RESET;
      TempCostObject.DELETEALL;

      IF TempCompany.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          Resource.RESET;
          IF ResourceWOP.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
            Resource.COPYFILTERS(ResourceWOP);
          Resource.SETRANGE(Company, COMPANYNAME);
          Resource.SETRANGE("Active in FSA", TRUE);
          IF Resource.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              CostObject.RESET;
              IF Resource."Filter Set (Mobile)" <> '' THEN
                ExportFilterSetMgtMobile.SetExportFiltersOnCostObject(
                  Resource."Filter Set (Mobile)", COMPANYNAME, CostObject);
              CostObject.FILTERGROUP(8);
              CostObject.SETRANGE("Dimension Code", GeneralLedgerSetup."Global Dimension 2 Code");
              CostObject.SETRANGE("Global Dimension No.", 2);
              CostObject.FILTERGROUP(0);
              IF CostObject.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  TempCostObject := CostObject;
                  IF NOT TempCostObject.FIND THEN
                    TempCostObject.INSERT;
                UNTIL CostObject.NEXT = 0;
            UNTIL Resource.NEXT = 0;
        UNTIL TempCompany.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillTempCostCode@1100409010();
    VAR
      CostCode@1100409000 : Record 11012083;
      Resource@1100409002 : Record 11229278;
      ExportFilterSetMgtMobile@1100409003 : Codeunit 11012200;
    BEGIN
      TempCostCode.RESET;
      TempCostCode.DELETEALL;

      IF TempCompany.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          Resource.RESET;
          IF ResourceWOP.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
            Resource.COPYFILTERS(ResourceWOP);
          Resource.SETRANGE(Company, COMPANYNAME);
          Resource.SETRANGE("Active in FSA", TRUE);
          IF Resource.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              CostCode.RESET;
              IF Resource."Filter Set (Mobile)" <> '' THEN
                ExportFilterSetMgtMobile.SetExportFiltersOnCostCode(
                  Resource."Filter Set (Mobile)", COMPANYNAME, CostCode);
              IF CostCode.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  TempCostCode := CostCode;
                  IF NOT TempCostCode.FIND THEN
                    TempCostCode.INSERT;
                UNTIL CostCode.NEXT = 0;
            UNTIL Resource.NEXT = 0;
        UNTIL TempCompany.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillTempWageComponent@1100409024();
    VAR
      WageComponent@1100409000 : Record 11012014;
      Resource@1100409002 : Record 11229278;
      ExportFilterSetMgtMobile@1100409003 : Codeunit 11012200;
    BEGIN
      TempWageComponent.RESET;
      TempWageComponent.DELETEALL;

      IF TempCompany.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          Resource.RESET;
          IF ResourceWOP.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
            Resource.COPYFILTERS(ResourceWOP);
          Resource.SETRANGE(Company, COMPANYNAME);
          Resource.SETRANGE("Active in FSA", TRUE);
          IF Resource.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              WageComponent.RESET;
              IF Resource."Filter Set (Mobile)" <> '' THEN
                ExportFilterSetMgtMobile.SetExportFiltersOnWageComp(
                  Resource."Filter Set (Mobile)", COMPANYNAME, WageComponent);
              WageComponent.FILTERGROUP(8);
              WageComponent.SETFILTER("Component Type", '%1|%2', WageComponent."Component Type"::Hours, WageComponent."Component Type"::Expenses);
              WageComponent.FILTERGROUP(0);
              IF WageComponent.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  TempWageComponent := WageComponent;
                  IF NOT TempWageComponent.FIND THEN
                    TempWageComponent.INSERT;
                UNTIL WageComponent.NEXT = 0;
            UNTIL Resource.NEXT = 0;
        UNTIL TempCompany.NEXT = 0;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared TotalPrinted As Boolean

Public Function LastRowIsTotal(ByVal Value As Boolean) As Boolean
    If TotalPrinted = False Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return False
    End If
    If TotalPrinted = True Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return True
    End If
End Function
</Code>
